World ^UzayYBS9

Network of networks ^53g6LM1a

Social networking or social networks in general are not really a new thing,
they have been around since the birth of the internet but the big change comes from
the ability to create a personal profile with your information and build a list
of friends that you can follow to see what happens in their lives. Not all lists are
created equals, sometimes the goals is to create an interconnection of friends
where you see them and they see you making it more bi-directional but other times
it is more about a group of people following the updates of a single person, similar
to a fan/celebrity relationship making it much more unidirectional ^F3fbH45Q

Facebook in now the most popular social
network and has reached what we call a
critical mass where it is so big the it became
self feeding and self sustaining ^zZp8VOLQ

LinkedIn is a career related social network, it is a 
place where people share their career progress and
can find job openings to candidate to. It is also
a great place where you can publicise your business
and gain clients ^0IFvkO3z

The concept of 6 degrees of separations is a scientist theory that applies to all social networks.
It states that the world is huge networks of smaller networks and because of this each person
is on a way at most 6 steps from any other person in the world ^Ygp9Ac2l

Twitter is a social network that is a bit different
from others, you still follow users or topics but what
you publish must be at most 140 characters, the equivalent
of a text message. This constant short updates create
what is called as the twitter stream, this can be considered
both asynchronous since the messages are saved but also
synchronous since it is so fast paced. Messages you
publish in the stream can also have mentions, hashtags and
can be retweeted by other further adding engagement to them.
You can also block users or contact them directly which
has no restrictions on the number of characters ^O9iNLmMo

Social media are not all benefits, they come with a very extensive sets of risks and dangers as well.
First of all they make personal information public, this infos can be used by others to impersonate
yourself and steal your identity to, for example, open a credit card in your name or ask your friends
for money. This is further enhanced by the fact that there is no real way to verify fully the identity
of someone online. One way to mitigate the problem is to be wary of which information you make available,
every social media has specific privacy settings that you should configure to make sure not too much info
is made public. Another danger is that social media might bring you to publish things that you would not
normally say openly, this is a danger because it might damage your reputation since employers usually
watch your profile during the interview process.
Another danger is that social media can cause addictions, so you feel like are not able to live without
them, this is especially dangerous when you get some following and you start to seek fame for the sake of
it, often leading to people "performing" only to please an audience. Another situation where addiction is even
more dangerous is when it is paired with bullying and trolling, this can make the person want to run away from
the offences but if your life depend on social medias you can not get off them and creates a very dangerous
situation. Another danger is that online information can spread much more rapidly than other types, this make
strong opinion much more viral than sometimes real facts and can lead to mass miss information. The last problem
comes from the funding of these websites, a great thing about them is that they are free to use but this comes
at the expenses of having to run ads on them, ads are not randomly showed but tailored to your interests. Other
than to your interests they are displayed in a way that maximise attention thanks to specific algorithms, these algos
are made to show you what you are more likely to feel engaged with and therefore in a way influence what you, know, 
experience, discover and even who you see. This is subjects to great critiques, and rightfully so, a and causes peoples
to only see things they already agree with limiting their view of the world. It is called the Filter bubble effect since it
is like you are close in a bubble and it also gain dangerousness when you pair it with the ability of false, but interesting
looking information spreading more easily than real once we discussed earlier.
Last but not leas, it is easy to notice how all these problems are very important but they are even more dangerous
when to use the platform are younger childs, this is why parents are alway recommended to supervise the use of social
networks ^YtOgUyoS
